Notice: Method of Information Collection

There are three or more methods to collect the information below.

1. The information may be collected from the professor when the professor announces the books used or notifies the students in class.

2. The information may be collected directly from the students who have knowledge of the textbooks used, or indirectly from the students - for instance, when a student asks for a question related to questions or information from a specific book.

3. The information may be collected from the lecture, which is graciously open to the curious minds of the public.

This page was able thanks to many who graciously contributed to the information and with the experience over time.

Thank you and best wishes to the journey of learning.
